				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Toccata and Fugue in D minor, BWV 565 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.25em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(238,232,170); width:65%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td align="center"><b>Authorship Note</b><br />Bach's authorship of this work is disputed.  See below, Comments.</td></tr></table></div>
<p><br />
</p>
<div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th>Incipit
</th>
<td>1. <img src="/images/lilypond/7a5df7d5d68b2b31a323872e8be7848e.png" alt="\relative c' { \clef treble \key d \minor \time 4/4 \tempo &quot;Adagio&quot; \compressFullBarRests&#10;a''8\mordent\fermata r32 g64 f e d cis32 d16 r r8\fermata a8\mordent\fermata r32 e f cis d16 r r8\fermata }" />
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>3 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1831
</td></tr>
<tr>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="Misc._Comments">Misc. Comments</span></h2>
<ul><li>One possible alternative author is <a href="/wiki/Category:Kellner,_Johann_Peter" title="Category:Kellner, Johann Peter">Johann Peter Kellner</a> (however, As Kellner was 3 years old in 1708, composition date should be regarded as quite uncertain really - Schissel &#160;)
</li><li>It may be that the Toccata and Fugue is based on an improvisation by Bach and noted down by one of his students.
</li><li>On the other hand, Grove Music does not consider this to be doubtful, although it has quite an extensive list of doubtful and spurious organ and keyboard works.
</li></ul>

</li><li><b>BWV 591</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Kleines_harmonisches_Labyrinth,_BWV_591_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Kleines harmonisches Labyrinth, BWV 591 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Kleines harmonisches Labyrinth</a></i> (doubtful; possibly by <a href="/wiki/Category:Heinichen,_Johann_David" title="Category:Heinichen, Johann David">Johann David Heinichen</a>)
</li><li><b>BWV 598</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/Pedal-Exercitium,_BWV_598_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Pedal-Exercitium, BWV 598 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Pedal-Exercitium</a></i> ("Pedal Exercise") (doubtful; possbily by <a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Carl_Philipp_Emanuel" title="Category:Bach, Carl Philipp Emanuel">Carl Philipp Emanuel Bach</a>)
</li><li><b>BWV 802-805</b> — <i><a href="/wiki/4_Duettos,_BWV_802-805_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="4 Duettos, BWV 802-805 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">4 Duettos</a></i> (from Clavierübung Volume III)
</li></ul>
</td></tr></table>
</td></tr></table>
